Setup conda enviroment\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWe created different conda enviroments for separating conflict tools.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTo create a conda content.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cem\u003eThey are separated because that telomerehunter use python2 and old version of others.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIt possible that you have already install libpng, but R can not find it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBecause it usually recongizes the libpng15.so, and you probably have another version.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSolution:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBefore running install_R_packages_RNAseq_quantTERRA.R\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake sure that there is libpng installed in your conda enviroment.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"conda install libpng \"\u003e\u003cpre class=\"notranslate\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003econda install libpng \n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003col start=\"2\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFind it under /your/path/to/anaconda3/env/your_env/lib/\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"For example. class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0"></div></div><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 etfROT"><section aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eRvpKx"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 cTsUqU js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-rna-seq_pipeline_quant_terra" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#rna-seq_pipeline_quant_terra"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>RNA-seq_pipeline_Quant_TERRA</h1>
<p dir="auto">This repo is a RNA-seq pipeline that can quantify TERRA expression level from different RNA-seq datasets downloaded from GEO database.</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-description" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#description"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Description</h2>
<p dir="auto">This pipeline is a combination of various bioinfomatic tools for performing reads dump, reads QC, alignment, total gene count and TERRA count. This pipeline inputs Sequence Read Archive (SRA) files and generates total gene and TERRA count tables for later expression analysis (For example, plotting heatmaps and boxplots).</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content--notice-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#-notice-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>** NOTICE **</h2>
<p dir="auto">The scripts provided in this pipeline were designed to be executed on computation nodes provided by National Center for High-performance Computing at Taiwan (NCHC Taiwan) using Slurm Queueing system. <em>Current version of scripts might not work on personal computer.</em></p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-terra-region-bed-files" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#terra-region-bed-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>TERRA region bed files</h2>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>The TERRA regions were defined based on RNA-seq reads mapping on CHM13 genome. The file is provided at: TERRA_RNA-seq_pipeline/CHM13_TERRA_region_v7.bed</li>
<li>A modified CHM13 cytobands file will be used in telomerehunter to quantify defined TERRA regions. The file is provided at: TERRA_RNA-seq_pipeline/chm13v2.0_cytobands_allchrs_Add_TERRA_v4.bed</li>
<li>For total human gene counts, we used gene annotation file provided by <a href="https://github.com/marbl/CHM13">CHM13 genome assembly</a> (Original cytoband file was downloaded from this page as well.)</li>
</ol>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-workflow" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#workflow"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Workflow</h2>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/153592683/296529150-b8e62fbf-e70d-4e6c-b573-6ecf0741be53.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3MDUzMDc4NzgsIm5iZiI6MTcwNTMwNzU3OCwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNTM1OTI2ODMvMjk2NTI5MTUwLWI4ZTYyZmJmLWU3MGQtNGU2Yy1iNTczLTZlY2YwNzQxYmU1My5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjQwMTE1JTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI0MDExNVQwODMyNThaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT04MTZjYTg3MDg2NzZkODZiN2U5NTczYTg2Y2E1MTgxZWI2ODk4MTUzMmFiMWEyZmI0MGRhZmM2NzZkMmIzYjcyJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCZhY3Rvcl9pZD0wJmtleV9pZD0wJnJlcG9faWQ9MCJ9.dV_9_9IcdgslmLtLfNCLZAEx58sRW5jnmzhF_RtwwSw"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/153592683/296529150-b8e62fbf-e70d-4e6c-b573-6ecf0741be53.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3MDUzMDc4NzgsIm5iZiI6MTcwNTMwNzU3OCwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNTM1OTI2ODMvMjk2NTI5MTUwLWI4ZTYyZmJmLWU3MGQtNGU2Yy1iNTczLTZlY2YwNzQxYmU1My5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjQwMTE1JTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI0MDExNVQwODMyNThaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT04MTZjYTg3MDg2NzZkODZiN2U5NTczYTg2Y2E1MTgxZWI2ODk4MTUzMmFiMWEyZmI0MGRhZmM2NzZkMmIzYjcyJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCZhY3Rvcl9pZD0wJmtleV9pZD0wJnJlcG9faWQ9MCJ9.dV_9_9IcdgslmLtLfNCLZAEx58sRW5jnmzhF_RtwwSw" alt="RNA-seq pipeline white" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-system-requirement" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#system-requirement"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>System Requirement</h2>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-hardware-requirement" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#hardware-requirement"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Hardware Requirement</h3>
<p dir="auto">The minimum requirements that can perfform STAR aligner should be enough to execute all tools in this pipeline.</p>
<p dir="auto">The requirements for STAR aligner are according to <a href="https://github.com/alexdobin/STAR">STAR Github page</a>.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Operation System: CentOS 7 or other later versions of Linux distrubutions.</li>
<li>CPU: x86-64 compatible processors</li>
<li>RAM: At least 16GB</li>
<li>Hard drive storage space: At lease 1TB</li>
</ol>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-software-requirement" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#software-requirement"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Software Requirement</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>SRAToolkit (v2.11.1)</li>
<li>TrimGalore (v0.6.3)</li>
<li>Cutadapt (v2.3)</li>
<li>fastqc (v0.12.1)</li>
<li>STAR (2.7.9a)</li>
<li>samtools (v1.13)</li>
<li>deeptools (v3.3.1)</li>
<li>htseq-count (2.0.3)</li>
<li>telomerehunter</li>
<li>Python version &gt;= 3.8</li>
<li>R version &gt;= 4.2</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Telomerehunter is used in this pipeline to calculate TERRA (or telomeric repeats) content of a RNA-seq dataset.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">*Reference paper: <a href="https://bmcbioinformatics.biomedcentral.com/articles/10.1186/s12859-019-2851-0#citeas" rel="nofollow"><em>Feuerbach, L., Sieverling, L., Deeg, K.I. et al. TelomereHunter  in silico estimation of telomere content and composition from cancer genomes. BMC Bioinformatics 20, 272 (2019).</em></a></p>
<h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-installation-guide" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#installation-guide"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Installation Guide</h1>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-1-download-this-pipeline" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#1-download-this-pipeline"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1. Download this pipeline</h2>
<p dir="auto">Directly download from this link: <a href="https://codeload.github.com/ls807terra/TERRA_RNA-seq_pipeline/zip/refs/heads/main">TERRA_RNA-seq_pipeline.zip</a></p>
<p dir="auto">or</p>
<p dir="auto">Download by git clone command: <code>git clone https://github.com/ls807terra/TERRA_RNA-seq_pipeline.git</code></p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-2-install-required-softwares" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#2-install-required-softwares"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2. <h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-3-setup-conda-enviroment" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#3-setup-conda-enviroment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>3. Setup conda enviroment</h2>
<p dir="auto">We created different conda enviroments for separating conflict tools.</p>
<p dir="auto">To create a conda enviroment as same as ours, use the yaml file provided in the <code>install_env/</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Two separated enviroment should be created!</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>RNAseq_quantTERRA_env</code> for general RNA-seq analysis.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>TelomereHunter_env</code> for counting telomeric-repeats read content.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><em>They are separated because that telomerehunter use python2 and old version of R.</em></p>
<p dir="auto"><em>The enviroment will crash if install telomerehunter with other tools.</em></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><em>Command line</em>:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>conda env create -n "RNAseq_quantTERRA_env" -f RNAseq_quantTERRA_env.yml</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>conda env create -n "TelomereHunter_env" -f TelomereHunter_env.yml</code></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-install-r-packages-for-rnaseq_quantterra_env" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#install-r-packages-for-rnaseq_quantterra_env"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Install R packages for <code>RNAseq_quantTERRA_env</code></h3>
<p dir="auto">All the package you need for the RNA-seq analysis (mainly DEseq2) can be install by executing the <code>install_R_packages_RNAseq_quantTERRA.R</code></p>
<p dir="auto">To install, first activate the conda enviroment:</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>conda activate RNAseq_quantTERRA_env</code></p>
<p dir="auto">Then execute the <strong>"install_R_packages_RNAseq_quantTERRA.R"</strong> by Rscript.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>Rscript install_R_packages_RNAseq_quantTERRA.R</code></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-install-r-packages-for-telomerehunter_env" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#install-r-packages-for-telomerehunter_env"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Install R packages for <code>TelomereHunter_env</code></h3>
<p dir="auto">Firstly, activate the conda enviroment:</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>conda activate TelomereHunter_env</code></p>
<p dir="auto">Then execute the <strong>"install_R_packages_TelomereHunter.R"</strong> by Rscript.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>Rscript install_R_packages_TelomereHunter.R</code></p>
<h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-run-this-pipeline" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#run-this-pipeline"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Run this pipeline</h1>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-1-download-sra-files-from-ncbi-database" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#1-download-sra-files-from-ncbi-database"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1. Download SRA files from NCBI database</h3>
<p dir="auto">First, you need to download the SRA files by SRAToolKit manually. Do this by the <code>prefetch</code> command.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>prefetch SRR_ID -o SRR_ID.sra</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><em><strong> This is because NCHC nodes are not allowed for connecting to the Internet.</strong></em></p>
<p dir="auto"><em><strong> Otherwise, it can be downloaded and exreacted to fastq by simply doing the command:</strong></em></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>fastq-dump --split-files SRR_ID -O /path/to/output/dir/</code></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-2-edit-the-pipeline-configure-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#2-edit-the-pipeline-configure-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2. Edit the pipeline configure file</h3>
<p dir="auto">Next, configure the <code>c.0_RNAseq_QuantTERRA.cfg</code> file.</p>
<p dir="auto">Edit the software path and other settings in the <code>c.0_RNAseq_QuantTERRA.cfg</code> file.</p>
<p dir="auto">After editing settings, run <code>sh 0_Configure_Setting.sh c.0_RNAseq_QuantTERRA.cfg</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>All pipeline scripts, <code>c.0_RNAseq_QuantTERRA.cfg</code> and <code>0_Configure_Setting.sh</code> should be under the same directory.</strong></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-3-execute-pipeline-this-will-run-on-computation-nodes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#3-execute-pipeline-this-will-run-on-computation-nodes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>3. Execute pipeline (This will run on computation nodes)</h3>
<p dir="auto"><strong><em>A series of jobs, including all steps in the pipeline, will be sent to computation nodes of NCHC Taiwania3 by Slurm queueing System.</em></strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Finally, sent a single SRA file to execute this pipeline by the following commands:**</p>
<p dir="auto"><em>Usage:</em> <code>sh 0.0_ps_Pipeline_v3.sh SRR_ID</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><em>Example:</em> <code>sh 0.0_ps_Pipeline_v3.sh SRRSRR3304509</code></p>
<h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-demo-and-data-reproduction" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#demo-and-data-reproduction"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Demo and Data reproduction</h1>
<p dir="auto">Here is a demonstration of using this pipeline, you can start from downloading SRA files from NCBI database or from processing fastq raw files.</p>
<p dir="auto">In the <strong><em>Demo</em></strong> folder, <code>SRA list.txt</code> records a series of SRA accession number that were used in the TERRA quantification of Figure3 in our paper. This demo describes steps to reproduce the result.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-start-from-downloading-sra-files" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#start-from-downloading-sra-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Start from downloading SRA files</h3>
<p dir="auto">First, download these data by SRAToolkit <code>prefetch</code> command or execute the script provided in this repository</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><em>command:</em></strong> <code>sh a.0_ps_SRA_download.sh Demo/SRA list.txt SRA</code></p>
<p dir="auto">This will download all SRA listed in the text file to <strong><em>SRA</em></strong> folder then downloaded SRA files can be fed into the pipeline.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Please named the folder as <code>SRA</code> and store SRA file in it to run the pipeline, current version of script does not recognize SRA folder in other name!</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Next, you can execute the pipeline script <code>0.0_ps_Pipeline_v4.sh</code> to process the SRA file one by one, for example:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><em>command:</em></strong> <code>sh 0.0_ps_Pipeline_v4.sh SRR7689162</code></p>
<p dir="auto">or execute by a loop:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><em>command:</em></strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="while read ln
 do
   sh 0.0_ps_Pipeline_v4.sh $ln
 done &lt; SRA list.txt"><pre class="notranslate"><code>while read ln
 do
   sh 0.0_ps_Pipeline_v4.sh $ln
 done &lt; SRA list.txt
</code></pre></div>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-expect-outputs" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#expect-outputs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Expect outputs</h2>
<p dir="auto">The raw data will process through the steps show in the <strong><em>Workflow</em></strong> diagram.</p>
<p dir="auto">Outputs from each step will be store at individule folder:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>folder</th>
<th align="center">file</th>
<th align="right">description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>fastq</td>
<td align="center">*.fastq.gz</td>
<td align="right">fastq files extract from a SRA file</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>trimed_fq</td>
<td align="center">*.fq.gz</td>
<td align="right">Adaptor and quailty trimmed fastq and QC files</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-start-from-fastq-files" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#start-from-fastq-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Start from fastq files</h3>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-normalize-conuts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#normalize-conuts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Normalize conuts</h2>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-plot-heatmaps-and-boxplots" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#plot-heatmaps-and-boxplots"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Plot heatmaps and boxplots</h2>
<h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-configure-file-format" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#configure-file-format"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Configure file format</h1>
<p dir="auto"><strong>The format of the configure file is as follow:</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="## Genome

# SRAToolKit prefetch

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-configure-files-rules" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#configure-files-rules"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Configure file's Rules</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Edit to change the softwares' paths, genome or Slurm settings, following the format of TOOL_NAME:/path/to/Software , separated by ":"</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">To register a new tool in configure file, Add a new line follow the format.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">To add a new tool and its path to pipeline:</p>
<p dir="auto">3.1 In the script of a new software (file name should follow this format: <em><em>ps</em></em>.sh), write:
''' software="TOOL_ID"
# To use the software
${software} -options [files] ... '''</p>
<p dir="auto">3.2 In the configure file, write:
''' TOOL_ID:/path/to/this/tool</p>
<p dir="auto">3.3 Run the script: <code>sh 0_Configure_Setting.sh this_configure_file.cfg</code>
This will reconginze the "TOOL_ID" in a script and replace it by "/path/to/this/tool"</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">To comment or annotate, please add a "#" at the start of a line.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Please update the software path if they were changed.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Make sure that all pipeline script (file name: <em><em>ps</em></em>.sh) are in the same directory with 0_Configure_Setting.sh and this configure file.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Notice!</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Your SRA file need to be locate at ${workdir}/SRA!</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Check the configure file <code>c.0_RNAseq_QuantTERRA.cfg</code>.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>The workdir is usually at "../" .</strong></p>
<h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-potential-problems-during-installation-and-run-time" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#potential-problems-during-installation-and-run-time"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Potential Problems during installation and run time</h1>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-notice-very-important" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#notice-very-important"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><strong>Notice! Very important!</strong></h3>
<p dir="auto">You will have some error when installing the R package <code>devtools</code> and <code>xml2</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">For solving  <code>xml2</code>, you simply need to install <code>libxml2</code> by conda, which is automaticlly installed by the yaml file.</p>
<p dir="auto">To handle <code>devtools</code> problem, you need to fix the libpng in the conda enviroment <code>lib/</code></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-problem1-libpng15-error" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#problem1-libpng15-error"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Problem1 libpng15 error:</h3>
<p dir="auto">libpng15 not found, when installing devtools and some others.</p>
<p dir="auto">It possible that you have already install libpng, but R can not find it.</p>
<p dir="auto">Because it usually recongizes the libpng15.so, and you probably have another version.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Before running install_R_packages_RNAseq_quantTERRA.R</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Make sure that there is libpng installed in your conda enviroment.</li>
</ol>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="conda install libpng "><pre class="notranslate"><code>conda install libpng 
</code></pre></div>
<ol start="2" dir="auto">
<li>Find it under /your/path/to/anaconda3/env/your_env/lib/</li>
</ol>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="For example. I have these file under my env path 

ls ~/anaconda3/env/TEST_env/lib/ | grep png

libpng16.a
libpng16.so
libpng16.so.16
libpng16.so.16.39.0
libpng.a
libpng.so

The version of my libpng is 16 not 15, so R can not find it."><pre class="notranslate"><code>For example. I have these file under my env path 

ls ~/anaconda3/env/TEST_env/lib/ | grep png

libpng16.a
libpng16.so
libpng16.so.16
libpng16.so.16.39.0
libpng.a
libpng.so

The version of my libpng is 16 not 15, so R can not find it.
</code></pre></div>
<ol start="3" dir="auto">
<li>Create a softlink that named "libpng15.so" but were direct to libpng16.so</li>
</ol>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Build a softlink 

ln -s libpng16.so.16.39.0 libpng15.so"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Build a softlink 

ln -s libpng16.so.16.39.0 libpng15.so
</code></pre></div>
<ol start="4" dir="auto">
<li>Now R should find libpng15 properly.</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Make sure the libpng were fixed. Then you can execute <code>install_R_packages_RNAseq_quantTERRA.R</code> by Rscript:</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>Rscript install_R_packages_RNAseq_quantTERRA.R</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><em>This will run a verrrrry long time.</em></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-problem2-run-time-error-of-telomerehunter" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#problem2-run-time-error-of-telomerehunter"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Problem2 Run time Error of telomerehunter:</h3>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Once you have install telomerehunter, you will probably find that it doesn't work.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This is because that you need to additionally install many R packages.</p>
<p dir="auto"><em>Strikingly, installing any version of R &gt;= 3.0 will crash this enviroment, you can only install those package under system.</em></p>
<p dir="auto"><em>If root permission was not avaliable, install it as a user R lib by specifying the install prefix to /home.</em></p>
<p dir="auto"><em>This will also run a verrrrry long time.</em></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-problem3-plot-pdf-bugs-of-telomerehunter" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#problem3-plot-pdf-bugs-of-telomerehunter"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Problem3 Plot PDF bugs of telomerehunter:</h3>
<p dir="auto">PDF plot have error while doing telomerehunter.</p>
<p dir="auto">It is because plenty of R script used in telomerehunter lacks <code>"library(ggplot2)"</code></p>
<p dir="auto">Therefore the error message often seem were <code>"there is no function ggplot()"</code> or <code>"there is no function theme()"</code></p>
<p dir="auto">To fix this, you need to find the R scritps of telomere hunter and edit them to add <code>"library(ggplot2)"</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">R script path:</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>/path/to/your/telomereHunter_env/lib/python2.7/site-packages/telomerehunter/</code></p>
<p dir="auto">Find those R scripts:</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>find /path/to/your/telomereHunter_env/* -name "*.R"</code></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="
For example, we have these R scripts:

telomereHunter/lib/python2.7/site-packages/telomerehunter/plot_gc_content_simple.R
telomereHunter/lib/python2.7/site-packages/telomerehunter/TVR_context_summary_tables.R
telomereHunter/lib/python2.7/site-packages/telomerehunter/plot_tel_content.R
telomereHunter/lib/python2.7/site-packages/telomerehunter/plot_repeat_frequency_intratelomeric.R

telomereHunter/lib/python2.7/site-packages/telomerehunter/plot_gc_content.R
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>
For example, we have these R scripts:

telomereHunter/lib/python2.7/site-packages/telomerehunter/plot_gc_content_simple.R
telomereHunter/lib/python2.7/site-packages/telomerehunter/TVR_context_summary_tables.R

<p dir="auto">Some of them have already load ggplot2 but some have not.</p>
<p dir="auto">Add "library(ggplot2)" to every R scripts is recommanded.</p>
<p dir="auto">After loading ggplot2, telomerehunter PDF plots can be generated.</p>
